  + CONTAINER_LOG_DIR=/var/log/containers/client
  + mkdir -p /var/log/containers/client
  + chmod 777 /var/log/containers/client
  + /opt/elasticbeanstalk/bin/log-conf -n applogs-client '-l/var/log/containers/client/*.log' -r size=1M,rotate=5
  + /opt/elasticbeanstalk/bin/log-conf -n applogs-client-rotated '-l/var/log/containers/client.log*' -t bundlelogs
  + for CONTAINER in '`cat $EB_CONFIG_APP_STAGING/Dockerrun.aws.json | jq -r .containerDefinitions[].name`'
  + CONTAINER_LOG_DIR=/var/log/containers/server
  + mkdir -p /var/log/containers/server
  + chmod 777 /var/log/containers/server
  + /opt/elasticbeanstalk/bin/log-conf -n applogs-server '-l/var/log/containers/server/*.log' -r size=1M,rotate=5
  + /opt/elasticbeanstalk/bin/log-conf -n applogs-server-rotated '-l/var/log/containers/server.log*' -t bundlelogs
  + for CONTAINER in '`cat $EB_CONFIG_APP_STAGING/Dockerrun.aws.json | jq -r .containerDefinitions[].name`'
  + CONTAINER_LOG_DIR=/var/log/containers/worker
  + mkdir -p /var/log/containers/worker
  + chmod 777 /var/log/containers/worker
  + /opt/elasticbeanstalk/bin/log-conf -n applogs-worker '-l/var/log/containers/worker/*.log' -r size=1M,rotate=5
  + /opt/elasticbeanstalk/bin/log-conf -n applogs-worker-rotated '-l/var/log/containers/worker.log*' -t bundlelogs
  + for CONTAINER in '`cat $EB_CONFIG_APP_STAGING/Dockerrun.aws.json | jq -r .containerDefinitions[].name`'
  + CONTAINER_LOG_DIR=/var/log/containers/nginx
  + mkdir -p /var/log/containers/nginx
